OBJECT Report 81659 Prognosis Overview IMT
{
  OBJECT-PROPERTIES
  {
    Date=;
    Time=;
    Version List=IM-REP-163;
  }
  PROPERTIES
  {
    CaptionML=[ENU=Prognosis Overview (new);
               NOR=Prognoseoversikt (ny);
               SVE=Prognosrapport (ny)];
    OnInitReport=BEGIN
                   ShowDetails := TRUE;
                 END;

    OnPreReport=BEGIN
                  CompanyInfo.GET;
                  CompanyInfo.CALCFIELDS(Picture);
                  SpecialCalcForCostComp := FALSE;
                END;

  }
  DATASET
  {
    { 1100285000;;DataItem;                  ;
               DataItemTable=Table11012034;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Project No.,Prognosis Date);
               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  Project.GET("Project No.");

                                  CASE Project."Forecast Level" OF
                                    Project."Forecast Level"::"Cost Component":
                                      BEGIN
                                        UseCostObject := FALSE;
                                        ShowDetails := FALSE;
                                        IF PrognosisLineCC.GET(Prognosis."Project No.",Prognosis."Prognosis Date", '7O') THEN
                                          SpecialCalcForCostComp := TRUE;
                                        TotalLbl := '';
                                      END;
                                    Project."Forecast Level"::"Cost Object":
                                      BEGIN
                                        UseCostObject := TRUE;
                                        TotalLbl := TotalTxt;
                                      END;
                                  END;

                                  Prognosis2.RESET;
                                  Prognosis2.SETRANGE("Project No.", "Project No.");
                                  Prognosis2.SETRANGE("Prognosis Date",0D,CALCDATE('-1D',"Prognosis Date"));
                                  IF Prognosis2.FINDLAST THEN
                                    PrevPrognDate := Prognosis2."Prognosis Date"
                                  ELSE
                                    PrevPrognDate := 0D;
                                  FillBuffer;
                                END;

               ReqFilterFields=Project No.,Prognosis Date }

    { 1100285003;1;Column;COMPANYNAME        ;
               SourceExpr=CompanyInfo.Name }

    { 1100285002;1;Column;CompanyPicture     ;
               SourceExpr=CompanyInfo.Picture }

    { 1100285005;1;Column;ProjectNo          ;
               IncludeCaption=Yes;
               SourceExpr="Project No." }

    { 1100285006;1;Column;PrognosisDate      ;
               IncludeCaption=Yes;
               SourceExpr="Prognosis Date" }

    { 1100285007;1;Column;ProjectDescription ;
               SourceExpr=Project.Description }

    { 1100285008;1;Column;PrognosisComment   ;
               IncludeCaption=Yes;
               SourceExpr=Comment }

    { 1100285127;1;Column;ShowNoBudget       ;
               SourceExpr=ShowNoBudget }

    { 1100285128;1;Column;UseCostObject      ;
               SourceExpr=UseCostObject }

    { 1000000001;1;Column;ContrAmt1          ;
               SourceExpr=ContrAmt[1] }

    { 1000000003;1;Column;ContrAmt2          ;
               SourceExpr=ContrAmt[2] }

    { 1000000002;1;Column;ContrAmt3          ;
               SourceExpr=ContrAmt[3] }

    { 1000000048;1;Column;PrevPrognDate      ;
               SourceExpr=PrevPrognDate }

    { 1000000049;1;Column;TotalLbl           ;
               SourceExpr=TotalLbl }

    { 1000000051;1;Column;ShowSpecialLine    ;
               SourceExpr=SpecialCalcForCostComp }

    { 1100285004;1;DataItem;                 ;
               DataItemTable=Table2000000026;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Number);
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               TmpPrognosisLine.RESET;

                               SETRANGE(Number,1,TmpPrognosisLine.COUNT);
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN

                                  IF Number = 1 THEN
                                    TmpPrognosisLine.FIND('-')
                                  ELSE
                                    TmpPrognosisLine.NEXT;
                                  TmpPrognosisLine.CALCFIELDS("Cost Object Description");
                                  ClearVars;
                                  WITH TmpPrognosisLine DO BEGIN
                                    IF "Cost Object" = '' THEN
                                      CurrReport.SKIP;

                                    // ITERO.KP 151214 >>
                                    IF (SpecialCalcForCostComp) AND ("Cost Type" = "Cost Type"::Sundry) THEN
                                      CurrReport.SKIP;
                                    // ITERO.KP 151214 <<
                                    IF "Cost Type"="Cost Type"::Revenue THEN
                                      Sign := 1
                                    ELSE
                                      Sign := -1;

                                    IF UseCostObject THEN BEGIN
                                      DimensionValue.SETRANGE(DimensionValue."Global Dimension No.",2);
                                      DimensionValue.SETRANGE(Code,"Cost Object");
                                      IF DimensionValue.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                                        CostComp := DimensionValue."Cost Component";
                                        CostComponent.GET(CostComp);
                                        CostCompDescription := CostComponent.Description;
                                      END;
                                    END ELSE BEGIN
                                      CostComp := "Cost Object";
                                      CostComponent.GET("Cost Object");
                                      CostCompDescription :=CostComponent.Description;
                                    END;
                                    HideHours := CostComponent."Cost Type" <> CostComponent."Cost Type"::Labor;
                                    // BUDGET >>
                                    // Initial Budget >>
                                    BudgetLine.RESET;
                                    BudgetLine.SETRANGE("Project No.","Project No.");
                                    BudgetLine.SETRANGE(Adjustment,'');
                                    BudgetLine.SETRANGE("Extension Contract",'');
                                    BudgetLine.SETRANGE("Version Date",0D,"Prognosis Date");
                                    BudgetLine.SETRANGE(Option,'');
                                    IF UseCostObject THEN
                                      BudgetLine.SETRANGE("Cost Object","Cost Object")
                                    ELSE
                                      BudgetLine.SETRANGE("Cost Component","Cost Object");

                                    BudgetLine.CALCSUMS("Amount (LCY)",Hours);
                                    OrgBudget[1]:=BudgetLine."Amount (LCY)" / 1000 * Sign;
                                    OrgBudgetH[1] := BudgetLine.Hours;
                                    // 151022 >>
                                    ProjectInstallment.RESET;
                                    ProjectInstallment.SETRANGE("Project No.", "Project No.");
                                    ProjectInstallment.SETFILTER("Extension Contract",'=%1','');
                                    IF UseCostObject THEN
                                      ProjectInstallment.SETRANGE("Cost Object","Cost Object")
                                    ELSE
                                      ProjectInstallment.SETRANGE("Cost Component","Cost Object");
                                    IF ProjectInstallment.FINDSET THEN REPEAT
                                      OrgBudget[1]+= ProjectInstallment."Installment Amount (LCY)" /1000 * Sign;
                                    UNTIL ProjectInstallment.NEXT=0;
                                    // 151022 <<
                                    // Adjustments >>
                                    BudgetLine.RESET;
                                    BudgetLine.SETRANGE("Project No.","Project No.");
                                    BudgetLine.SETFILTER(Adjustment,'<>%1','');
                                    BudgetLine.SETRANGE("Extension Contract",'');
                                    BudgetLine.SETRANGE("Version Date",0D,"Prognosis Date");
                                    BudgetLine.SETRANGE(Option,'');
                                    IF UseCostObject THEN
                                      BudgetLine.SETRANGE("Cost Object","Cost Object")
                                    ELSE
                                      BudgetLine.SETRANGE("Cost Component","Cost Object");

                                    BudgetLine.CALCSUMS("Amount (LCY)",Hours);
                                    Adjustment[1] :=BudgetLine."Amount (LCY)" / 1000 * Sign;
                                    AdjustmentsH[1] := BudgetLine.Hours;
                                    // Extensions >>
                                    BudgetLine.RESET;
                                    BudgetLine.SETRANGE("Project No.","Project No.");
                                    BudgetLine.SETRANGE(Adjustment,'');
                                    BudgetLine.SETFILTER("Extension Contract",'<>%1','');
                                    BudgetLine.SETRANGE("Version Date",0D,"Prognosis Date");
                                    BudgetLine.SETFILTER("Extension Contract Status",'%1|%2',
                                          BudgetLine."Extension Contract Status"::Order,
                                          BudgetLine."Extension Contract Status"::"Invoicing Allowed");
                                    BudgetLine.SETRANGE(Option,'');
                                    IF UseCostObject THEN
                                      BudgetLine.SETRANGE("Cost Object","Cost Object")
                                    ELSE
                                      BudgetLine.SETRANGE("Cost Component","Cost Object");

                                    BudgetLine.CALCSUMS("Amount (LCY)",Hours);
                                    Extensions[1]:=BudgetLine."Amount (LCY)" / 1000 * Sign;
                                    ExtensionsH[1] := BudgetLine.Hours;
                                    // 151022 >>
                                    ProjectInstallment.SETFILTER("Extension Contract",'<>%1','');
                                    IF UseCostObject THEN
                                      ProjectInstallment.SETRANGE("Cost Object","Cost Object")
                                    ELSE
                                      ProjectInstallment.SETRANGE("Cost Component","Cost Object");
                                    IF ProjectInstallment.FINDSET THEN REPEAT
                                      Extensions[1]+= ProjectInstallment."Installment Amount (LCY)" /1000 * Sign;
                                    UNTIL ProjectInstallment.NEXT=0;
                                    // 151022 <<

                                    // BUDGET <<

                                    // ACTUAL / Upparbetat >>
                                    JobLedgerEntry.SETCURRENTKEY("Job No.", "Posting Date");
                                    JobLedgerEntry.SETRANGE("Job No.","Project No.");
                                   // JobLedgerEntry.SETRANGE("Posting Date",0D,"Prognosis Date");     WVG  No date filter on actual
                                    IF UseCostObject THEN
                                      JobLedgerEntry.SETRANGE("Global Dimension 2 Code","Cost Object")
                                    ELSE
                                      JobLedgerEntry.SETRANGE("Cost Component","Cost Object");

                                    //JobLedgerEntry.SETRANGE("Entry Type",JobLedgerEntry."Entry Type"::Usage);
                                    IF JobLedgerEntry.FIND('-') THEN REPEAT
                                        CASE JobLedgerEntry."Entry Type" OF
                                          JobLedgerEntry."Entry Type"::Usage : ActualPosted[1] += JobLedgerEntry."Total Cost (LCY)" * Sign / 1000;
                                          JobLedgerEntry."Entry Type"::Sale : ActualPosted[1] += JobLedgerEntry."Total Price (LCY)" * Sign * -1 / 1000;
                                        END;

                                        IF "Cost Type" = "Cost Type"::Labor THEN
                                          ActualHours[1] += JobLedgerEntry.Quantity;
                                    UNTIL JobLedgerEntry.NEXT=0;

                                    HourAccLine.SETCURRENTKEY("Project No.","Cost Type","Cost Object","Posting Date");
                                    HourAccLine.SETRANGE("Project No.","Project No.");
                                    IF UseCostObject THEN
                                      HourAccLine.SETRANGE("Cost Object","Cost Object")
                                    ELSE
                                      HourAccLine.SETRANGE("Cost Component","Cost Object");
                                  //  HourAccLine.SETRANGE("Posting Date",0D,"Prognosis Date");             WVG   No date filter on actual
                                    IF HourAccLine.FIND('-') THEN REPEAT
                                      ActualHours[1] += HourAccLine."Total Line";
                                    UNTIL HourAccLine.NEXT=0;

                                    PurchControlLine.SETCURRENTKEY("Project No.",Date);
                                    PurchControlLine.SETRANGE("Project No." ,"Project No.");
                                    IF UseCostObject THEN
                                      PurchControlLine.SETRANGE("Shortcut Dimension 2 Code","Cost Object")
                                    ELSE
                                      PurchControlLine.SETRANGE("Cost Component","Cost Object");

                                    //PurchControlLine.SETRANGE(Date,0D,"Prognosis Date");                 WVG  No date filter on actual
                                    IF PurchControlLine.FIND('-') THEN REPEAT
                                      ActualOpen[1] += (PurchControlLine."Outstanding Amount" + PurchControlLine."Amt. Rcd. Not Invoiced")* Sign / 1000;
                                    UNTIL PurchControlLine.NEXT=0;
                                    // ACTUAL / Upparbetat <<

                                    IF UseCostObject THEN BEGIN
                                      IF PrevPrognDate <> 0D THEN BEGIN
                                        PrognosisLine2.RESET;
                                        PrognosisLine2.SETRANGE("Project No.","Project No.");
                                        PrognosisLine2.SETRANGE("Prognosis Date", PrevPrognDate);
                                        PrognosisLine2.SETRANGE("Cost Object","Cost Object");
                                        IF PrognosisLine2.FINDSET THEN REPEAT
                                          PrevCost[1] += (PrognosisLine2."Prognosis Total Cost" +
                                              PrognosisLine2."Amount Revenue" + PrognosisLine2.Invoiced ) * Sign / 1000;  // 151022
                                          PrevHours[1] += PrognosisLine2."Prognosis Total Hours";
                                        UNTIL PrognosisLine2.NEXT=0;

                                      END;
                                    END ELSE BEGIN
                                      IF PrevPrognDate <> 0D THEN BEGIN
                                        PrognosisLine2CC.RESET;
                                        PrognosisLine2CC.SETRANGE("Project No.","Project No.");
                                        PrognosisLine2CC.SETRANGE("Prognosis Date", PrevPrognDate);
                                        PrognosisLine2CC.SETRANGE("Cost Component Code","Cost Object");
                                        PrognosisLine2CC.CALCSUMS("Prognosis Total Revenues","Prognosis Total Cost","Prognosis Total Hours");
                                        PrevCost[1] := (PrognosisLine2CC."Prognosis Total Revenues" + PrognosisLine2CC."Prognosis Total Cost") * Sign / 1000;
                                        PrevHours[1] := PrognosisLine2CC."Prognosis Total Hours";
                                      END;
                                    END;


                                    NewHours[1] := "Prognosis Total Hours";
                                    IF UseCostObject THEN
                                      NewRemaining[1] := (Amount + "Amount Revenue") * Sign/1000
                                    ELSE BEGIN
                                      PrognosisLine2CC.GET("Project No.","Prognosis Date","Cost Object");
                                      //NewRemaining[1] := (PrognosisLine2CC."Prognosis Total Costs" + PrognosisLine2CC."Prognosis Total Revenue") * Sign/1000;
                                      NewRemaining[1] := (PrognosisLine2CC."Prognosis Costs" + PrognosisLine2CC."Prognosis Amount Revenue") * Sign/1000;
                                    END;

                                    IF UseCostObject THEN BEGIN
                                      IF Sign = 1 THEN // Revenue
                                        NewTotal[1] :=  ("Prognosis Total Cost" + Invoiced) / 1000 * Sign //NewRemaining[1] + ActualPosted[1] + ActualOpen[1]; 151022
                                      ELSE
                                        NewTotal[1] := ("Prognosis Total Cost" + Invoiced - Amount) / 1000 * Sign;

                                      NewTotal[1] += NewRemaining[1];

                                    END ELSE BEGIN
                                      PrognosisLine2CC.GET("Project No.","Prognosis Date","Cost Object");
                                      NewTotal[1] := (PrognosisLine2CC."Prognosis Total Cost" + PrognosisLine2CC."Prognosis Total Revenues") /1000 * Sign;
                                    END;

                                    IF "Cost Type" = "Cost Type"::Revenue THEN BEGIN
                                        OrgBudget[4] += OrgBudget[1];
                                        OrgBudgetH[4] += OrgBudgetH[1];
                                        Adjustment[4] += Adjustment[1];
                                        ActualPosted[4] += ActualPosted[1];
                                        ActualHours[4] += ActualHours[1];
                                        ActualOpen[4] +=ActualOpen[1];
                                        Adjustment[4] += Adjustment[1];
                                        AdjustmentsH[4] +=AdjustmentsH[1];
                                        Extensions[4]+= Extensions[1];
                                        ExtensionsH[4] += ExtensionsH[1];
                                        PrevCost[4] += PrevCost[1];
                                        PrevHours[4] += PrevHours[1];
                                        NewTotal[4] += NewTotal[1];
                                        NewHours[4] += NewHours[1];
                                        NewRemaining[4] += NewRemaining[1];
                                    END;
                                    IF UseCostObject THEN BEGIN
                                      IF "Cost Object" IN ['9901','9903','9998','9999'] THEN BEGIN
                                        IF "Cost Object" = '9901' THEN BEGIN
                                          CostObjDescr[2] := STRSUBSTNO('%1 %2',"Cost Object","Cost Object Description");
                                          OrgBudget[2] += OrgBudget[1];
                                          OrgBudgetH[2] += OrgBudgetH[1];
                                          Adjustment[2] += Adjustment[1];
                                          ActualPosted[2] += ActualPosted[1];
                                          ActualHours[2] += ActualHours[1];
                                          ActualOpen[2] +=ActualOpen[1];
                                          Adjustment[2] += Adjustment[1];
                                          AdjustmentsH[2] +=AdjustmentsH[1];
                                          Extensions[2] += Extensions[1];
                                          ExtensionsH[2] += ExtensionsH[1];
                                          PrevCost [2] += PrevCost[1];
                                          PrevHours[2] += PrevHours[1];
                                          NewTotal[2] += NewTotal[1];
                                          NewHours[2] += NewHours[1];
                                          NewRemaining[2] += NewRemaining[1];
                                        END;
                                        IF "Cost Object" = '9903' THEN BEGIN
                                          CostObjDescr[3] := STRSUBSTNO('%1 %2',"Cost Object","Cost Object Description");
                                          OrgBudget[3] += OrgBudget[1];
                                          OrgBudgetH[3] += OrgBudgetH[1];
                                          Adjustment[3] += Adjustment[1];
                                          ActualPosted[3] += ActualPosted[1];
                                          ActualHours[3] += ActualHours[1];
                                          ActualOpen[3] +=ActualOpen[1];
                                          Adjustment[3] += Adjustment[1];
                                          AdjustmentsH[3] +=AdjustmentsH[1];
                                          Extensions[3]+= Extensions[1];
                                          ExtensionsH[3] += ExtensionsH[1];
                                          PrevCost [3] += PrevCost[1];
                                          PrevHours[3] += PrevHours[1];
                                          NewTotal[3] += NewTotal[1];
                                          NewHours[3] += NewHours[1];
                                          NewRemaining[3] += NewRemaining[1];
                                        END;
                                        IF "Cost Object" = '9998' THEN BEGIN
                                          CostObjDescr[8] := STRSUBSTNO('%1 %2',"Cost Object","Cost Object Description");
                                          OrgBudget[8] += OrgBudget[1];
                                          OrgBudgetH[8] += OrgBudgetH[1];
                                          Adjustment[8] += Adjustment[1];
                                          ActualPosted[8] += ActualPosted[1];
                                          ActualHours[8] += ActualHours[1];
                                          ActualOpen[8] +=ActualOpen[1];
                                          Adjustment[8] += Adjustment[1];
                                          AdjustmentsH[8] +=AdjustmentsH[1];
                                          Extensions[8]+= Extensions[1];
                                          ExtensionsH[8] += ExtensionsH[1];
                                          PrevCost [8] += PrevCost[1];
                                          PrevHours[8] += PrevHours[1];
                                          NewTotal[8] += NewTotal[1];
                                          NewHours[8] += NewHours[1];
                                          NewRemaining[8] += NewRemaining[1];
                                        END;
                                        IF "Cost Object" = '9999' THEN BEGIN
                                          CostObjDescr[9] := STRSUBSTNO('%1 %2',"Cost Object","Cost Object Description");
                                          OrgBudget[9] += OrgBudget[1];
                                          OrgBudgetH[9] += OrgBudgetH[1];
                                          Adjustment[9] += Adjustment[1];
                                          ActualPosted[9] += ActualPosted[1];
                                          ActualHours[9] += ActualHours[1];
                                          ActualOpen[9] +=ActualOpen[1];
                                          Adjustment[9] += Adjustment[1];
                                          AdjustmentsH[9] +=AdjustmentsH[1];
                                          Extensions[9]+= Extensions[1];
                                          ExtensionsH[9] += ExtensionsH[1];
                                          PrevCost [9] += PrevCost[1];
                                          PrevHours[9] += PrevHours[1];
                                          NewTotal[9] += NewTotal[1];
                                          NewHours[9] += NewHours[1];
                                          NewRemaining[9] += NewRemaining[1];
                                        END;
                                       CurrReport.SKIP
                                      END ELSE BEGIN
                                        OrgBudget[5] += OrgBudget[1];
                                        OrgBudgetH[5] += OrgBudgetH[1];
                                        Adjustment[5] += Adjustment[1];
                                        ActualPosted[5] += ActualPosted[1];
                                        ActualHours[5] += ActualHours[1];
                                        ActualOpen[5] +=ActualOpen[1];
                                        Adjustment[5] += Adjustment[1];
                                        AdjustmentsH[5] +=AdjustmentsH[1];
                                        Extensions[5]+= Extensions[1];
                                        ExtensionsH[5] += ExtensionsH[1];
                                        PrevCost[5] += PrevCost[1];
                                        PrevHours[5] += PrevHours[1];
                                        NewTotal[5] += NewTotal[1];
                                        NewHours[5] += NewHours[1];
                                        NewRemaining[5] += NewRemaining[1];
                                      END;
                                    END ELSE BEGIN
                                      OrgBudget[5] += OrgBudget[1];
                                      OrgBudgetH[5] += OrgBudgetH[1];
                                      Adjustment[5] += Adjustment[1];
                                      ActualPosted[5] += ActualPosted[1];
                                      ActualHours[5] += ActualHours[1];
                                      ActualOpen[5] +=ActualOpen[1];
                                      Adjustment[5] += Adjustment[1];
                                      AdjustmentsH[5] +=AdjustmentsH[1];
                                      Extensions[5]+= Extensions[1];
                                      ExtensionsH[5] += ExtensionsH[1];
                                      PrevCost[5] += PrevCost[1];
                                      PrevHours[5] += PrevHours[1];
                                      NewTotal[5] += NewTotal[1];
                                      NewHours[5] += NewHours[1];
                                      NewRemaining[5] += NewRemaining[1];
                                    END;

                                    CLEAR(ContrAmt);
                                    ProjectPrincipal.RESET;
                                    ProjectPrincipal.SETAUTOCALCFIELDS("Total Extension Contract");
                                    ProjectPrincipal.SETRANGE("Project No.","Project No.");
                                    IF ProjectPrincipal.FINDSET THEN REPEAT
                                      ContrAmt[1] += ProjectPrincipal."Contract Amount (LCY)" / 1000;
                                      ContrAmt[2] += ProjectPrincipal."Total Extension Contract" / 1000;

                                    UNTIL ProjectPrincipal.NEXT=0;
                                    ContrAmt[3] += ContrAmt[1] + ContrAmt[2];
                                  END;
                                END;
                                 }

    { 1100285129;2;Column;HideHours          ;
               SourceExpr=HideHours }

    { 1100285019;2;Column;ShowDetails        ;
               SourceExpr=ShowDetails }

    { 1100285009;2;Column;CostType_PrognosisLine;
               SourceExpr=TmpPrognosisLine."Cost Type" }

    { 1100285010;2;Column;CostObject_PrognosisLine;
               SourceExpr=TmpPrognosisLine."Cost Object" }

    { 1100285011;2;Column;CostObjectDescription_PrognosisLine;
               SourceExpr=TmpPrognosisLine."Cost Object Description" }

    { 1100285012;2;Column;CostComponent      ;
               SourceExpr=CostComp }

    { 1100285013;2;Column;CostCompDescription;
               SourceExpr=CostCompDescription }

    { 1100285015;2;Column;Adjustments        ;
               SourceExpr=Adjustment[1] }

    { 1100285017;2;Column;AdjustmentH        ;
               SourceExpr=AdjustmentsH[1] }

    { 1100285016;2;Column;OriginalBudget     ;
               SourceExpr=OrgBudget[1] }

    { 1100285018;2;Column;OriginalBudgetH    ;
               SourceExpr=OrgBudgetH[1] }

    { 1100285014;2;Column;Extensions         ;
               SourceExpr=Extensions[1] }

    { 1100285020;2;Column;ExtensionsH        ;
               SourceExpr=ExtensionsH[1] }

    { 1100285021;2;Column;ActualPosted       ;
               SourceExpr=ActualPosted[1] }

    { 1100285022;2;Column;ActualHours        ;
               SourceExpr=ActualHours[1] }

    { 1100285023;2;Column;ActualOpen         ;
               SourceExpr=ActualOpen[1] }

    { 1100285024;2;Column;PrevCost           ;
               SourceExpr=PrevCost[1] }

    { 1100285025;2;Column;PrevHours          ;
               SourceExpr=PrevHours[1] }

    { 1100285026;2;Column;NewTotal           ;
               SourceExpr=NewTotal[1] }

    { 1100285027;2;Column;NewHours           ;
               SourceExpr=NewHours[1] }

    { 1100285028;2;Column;NewRemaining       ;
               SourceExpr=NewRemaining[1] }

    { 1100285033;1;DataItem;TotalsLoop       ;
               DataItemTable=Table2000000026;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Number)
                                 ORDER(Ascending);
               MaxIteration=1;
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN

                               SpecialCalcForCostComponent;

                               // [4] is revenue
                               // [5] is totals without the four cost objects
                               OrgBudget[4] := OrgBudget[4] ;//+ ContrAmt[1];
                               OrgBudget[6] := OrgBudget[6] ;//+ ContrAmt[1];
                               OrgBudget[7] := OrgBudget[7] ;//+ ContrAmt[1];
                               Extensions[4] := Extensions[4] ;//+ ContrAmt[2];
                               Extensions[6] := Extensions[6] ;//+ ContrAmt[2];
                               Extensions[7] := Extensions[7] ;//+ ContrAmt[2];

                               Assign(OrgBudget[6],OrgBudget[4]);
                               Assign(OrgBudgetH[6],OrgBudgetH[4]);
                               Assign(Adjustment[6],Adjustment[4]);
                               Assign(ActualPosted[6],ActualPosted[4]);
                               Assign(ActualHours[6],ActualHours[4]);
                               Assign(ActualOpen[6],ActualOpen[4]);
                               Assign(Adjustment[6],Adjustment[4]);
                               Assign(AdjustmentsH[6],AdjustmentsH[4]);
                               Assign(Extensions[6],Extensions[4]);
                               Assign(ExtensionsH[6],ExtensionsH[4]);
                               Assign(PrevCost[6],PrevCost[4]);
                               Assign(PrevHours[6],PrevHours[4]);
                               Assign(NewTotal[6],NewTotal[4]);
                               Assign(NewHours[6],NewHours[4]);
                               Assign(NewRemaining[6],NewRemaining[4]);


                               Assign(OrgBudget[7],OrgBudget[4]);
                               Assign(OrgBudgetH[7],OrgBudgetH[4]);
                               Assign(Adjustment[7],Adjustment[4]);
                               Assign(ActualPosted[7],ActualPosted[4]);
                               Assign(ActualHours[7],ActualHours[4]);
                               Assign(ActualOpen[7],ActualOpen[4]);
                               Assign(Adjustment[7],Adjustment[4]);
                               Assign(AdjustmentsH[7],AdjustmentsH[4]);
                               Assign(Extensions[7],Extensions[4]);
                               Assign(ExtensionsH[7],ExtensionsH[4]);
                               Assign(PrevCost[7],PrevCost[4]);
                               Assign(PrevHours[7],PrevHours[4]);
                               Assign(NewTotal[7],NewTotal[4]);
                               Assign(NewHours[7],NewHours[4]);
                               Assign(NewRemaining[7],NewRemaining[4]);


                               BudgetTotalPct := OrgBudget[4] + Adjustment[4] + Extensions[4];
                               Divide( OrgBudget[5] + Adjustment[5] + Extensions[5],BudgetTotalPct); // ContrAmt[3] +

                               ActualTotalPct := ActualPosted[4] + ActualOpen[4];
                               Divide(ActualPosted[5] + ActualOpen[5],ActualTotalPct);

                               Divide(OrgBudget[5] ,OrgBudget[4]); // + ContrAmt[1]
                               Divide(OrgBudgetH[5],OrgBudgetH[4]);
                               Divide(Adjustment[5]+OrgBudget[5],Adjustment[4]);
                               Divide(ActualPosted[5],ActualPosted[4]);
                               Divide(ActualHours[5],ActualHours[4]);
                               Divide(ActualOpen[5],ActualOpen[4]);
                               Divide(Adjustment[5],Adjustment[4]);
                               Divide(AdjustmentsH[5],AdjustmentsH[4]);
                               Divide(Extensions[5] ,Extensions[4]); // + ContrAmt[2]
                               Divide(ExtensionsH[5],ExtensionsH[4]);
                               Divide(PrevCost[5],PrevCost[4]);
                               Divide(PrevHours[5],PrevHours[4]);
                               Divide(NewTotal[5],NewTotal[4]);
                               Divide(NewHours[5],NewHours[4]);
                               Divide(NewRemaining[5],NewRemaining[4]);


                               BudgetTotalPct2 := OrgBudget[6] + Adjustment[6] + Extensions[6];
                               Divide(OrgBudget[5] + Adjustment[5] + Extensions[5] +   // ContrAmt[3] +
                                      OrgBudget[2] + Adjustment[2] + Extensions[2] +
                                      OrgBudget[8] + Adjustment[8] + Extensions[8],BudgetTotalPct2);

                               ActualTotalPct2 := ActualPosted[6] + ActualOpen[6];
                               Divide(ActualPosted[5] + ActualOpen[5] +
                                      ActualPosted[2] + ActualOpen[2] +
                                      ActualPosted[8] + ActualOpen[8], ActualTotalPct2);

                               Divide( OrgBudget[5]    + OrgBudget[2]    + OrgBudget[8]    ,OrgBudget[6]); // ContrAmt[1] +
                               Divide(OrgBudgetH[5]   + OrgBudgetH[2]   + OrgBudgetH[8]   ,OrgBudgetH[6]);
                               Divide(Adjustment[5]  + Adjustment[2]  + Adjustment[8] + OrgBudget[2] + OrgBudget[8],Adjustment[6]);
                               Divide(ActualPosted[5] + ActualPosted[2] + ActualPosted[8] ,ActualPosted[6]);
                               Divide(ActualHours[5]  + ActualHours[2]  + ActualHours[8]  ,ActualHours[6]);
                               Divide(ActualOpen[5]   + ActualOpen[2]   + ActualOpen[8]   ,ActualOpen[6]);
                               Divide(Adjustment[5]  + Adjustment[2]  + Adjustment[8]  ,Adjustment[6]);
                               Divide(AdjustmentsH[5] + AdjustmentsH[2] + AdjustmentsH[8] ,AdjustmentsH[6]);
                               Divide( Extensions[5]   + Extensions[2]   + Extensions[8]   ,Extensions[6]); // ContrAmt[2] +
                               Divide(ExtensionsH[5]  + ExtensionsH[2]  + ExtensionsH[8]  ,ExtensionsH[6]);
                               Divide(PrevCost[5]     + PrevCost[2]     + PrevCost[8]     ,PrevCost[6]);
                               Divide(PrevHours[5]    + PrevHours[2]    + PrevHours[8]    ,PrevHours[6]);
                               Divide(NewTotal[5]     + NewTotal[2]     + NewTotal[8]     ,NewTotal[6]);
                               Divide(NewHours[5]     + NewHours[2]     + NewHours[8]     ,NewHours[6]);
                               Divide(NewRemaining[5] + NewRemaining[2] + NewRemaining[8] ,NewRemaining[6]);

                               BudgetTotalPct3 := OrgBudget[7] + Adjustment[7] + Extensions[7];
                               Divide( // ContrAmt[3] +
                                      OrgBudget[5] + Adjustment[5] + Extensions[5] +
                                      OrgBudget[3] + Adjustment[3] + Extensions[3] +
                                      OrgBudget[2] + Adjustment[2] + Extensions[2] +
                                      OrgBudget[8] + Adjustment[8] + Extensions[8] +
                                      OrgBudget[9] + Adjustment[9] + Extensions[9] +
                                      OrgBudgetS + AdjustmentsS + ExtensionsS ,BudgetTotalPct3);

                               ActualTotalPct3 := ActualPosted[7] + ActualOpen[7];
                               Divide(ActualPosted[5] + ActualOpen[5] +
                                      ActualPosted[3] + ActualOpen[3] +
                                      ActualPosted[2] + ActualOpen[2] +
                                      ActualPosted[8] + ActualOpen[8] +
                                      ActualPosted[9] + ActualOpen[9] +
                                      ActualOpenS + ActualPostedS, ActualTotalPct3);

                               Divide(OrgBudget[5]   + OrgBudget[2]  + OrgBudget[3]    + OrgBudget[8] + OrgBudget[9] +
                                       OrgBudgetS, OrgBudget[7]); // ContrAmt[1] +
                               Divide(OrgBudgetH[5]  + OrgBudgetH[2] + OrgBudgetH[3]   + OrgBudgetH[8] + OrgBudgetH[9],OrgBudgetH[7]);

                               Divide(Adjustment[5] + Adjustment[2] + Adjustment[3] + Adjustment[8] + Adjustment[9] +
                                      OrgBudget[5]   + OrgBudget[2]   + OrgBudget[3]   + OrgBudget[8]   + OrgBudget[9] +
                                      AdjustmentsS + OrgBudgetS,Adjustment[7]);

                               Divide(ActualPosted[5] + ActualPosted[2] + ActualPosted[3] + ActualPosted[8]
                                       + ActualPosted[9] + ActualPostedS ,ActualPosted[7]);
                               Divide(ActualHours[5]  + ActualHours[2]  + ActualHours[3]  + ActualHours[8]  + ActualHours[9]  ,ActualHours[7]);
                               Divide(ActualOpen[5]   + ActualOpen[2]   + ActualOpen[3]   + ActualOpen[8]
                                       + ActualOpen[9] + ActualOpenS, ActualOpen[7]);
                               Divide(Adjustment[5]  + Adjustment[2]  + Adjustment[3]  + Adjustment[8]  + Adjustment[9]  ,Adjustment[7]);
                               Divide(AdjustmentsH[5] + AdjustmentsH[2] + AdjustmentsH[3] + AdjustmentsH[8] + AdjustmentsH[9] ,AdjustmentsH[7]);
                               Divide(Extensions[5]   + Extensions[2]   + Extensions[3]   + Extensions[8]   + Extensions[9]
                                       + ExtensionsS, Extensions[7]); // ContrAmt[2] +
                               Divide(ExtensionsH[5]  + ExtensionsH[2]  + ExtensionsH[3]  + ExtensionsH[8]  + ExtensionsH[9]  ,ExtensionsH[7]);
                               Divide(PrevCost[5]     + PrevCost[2]     + PrevCost[3]     + PrevCost[8]     +
                                       PrevCost[9] + PrevCostS    ,PrevCost[7]);
                               Divide(PrevHours[5]    + PrevHours[2]    + PrevHours[3]    + PrevHours[8]    + PrevHours[9]    ,PrevHours[7]);
                               Divide(NewTotal[5]     + NewTotal[2]     + NewTotal[3]     + NewTotal[8]     +
                                       NewTotal[9] + NewTotalS     ,NewTotal[7]);
                               Divide(NewHours[5]     + NewHours[2]     + NewHours[3]     + NewHours[8]     + NewHours[9]     ,NewHours[7]);
                               Divide(NewRemaining[5] + NewRemaining[2] + NewRemaining[3] + NewRemaining[8] +
                                       NewRemaining[9] + NewRemainingS,NewRemaining[7]);
                             END;
                              }

      PrevCost@1100285015 : ARRAY [10] OF Decimal;
      PrevCostS@1000000013 : Decimal;
      PrevHours@1100285024 : ARRAY [10] OF Decimal;
      NewTotal@1100285026 : ARRAY [10] OF Decimal;
      NewTotalS@1000000014 : Decimal;
      NewHours@1100285030 : ARRAY [10] OF Decimal;
      NewRemaining@1100285031 : ARRAY [10] OF Decimal;
      NewRemainingS@1000000015 : Decimal;
      BudgetTotalPct@1100285025 : Decimal;
      ActualTotalPct@1100285027 : Decimal;
      BudgetTotalPct2@1100285032 : Decimal;
      ActualTotalPct2@1100285029 : Decimal;
      BudgetTotalPct3@1100285034 : Decimal;
      ActualTotalPct3@1100285033 : Decimal;
      ShowDetails@1100285003 : Boolean;
      ShowNoBudget@1000000010 : Boolean;
      UseCostObject@1000000005 : Boolean;
      HideHours@1100285037 : Boolean;
      SpecialCalcForCostComp@1000000012 : Boolean;
      ContrAmt@1000000002 : ARRAY [3] OF Decimal;
      PrintOnce@1000000003 : Integer;
      CostObjDescr@1100285028 : ARRAY [10] OF Text;
      counter@1000000009 : Integer;
      TotalTxt@1000000021 : TextConst 'ENU=Total;NOR=Sum;SVE=Summa';

    PROCEDURE FillBuffer@1000000002();
    BEGIN

      TmpPrognosisLine.RESET;
      TmpPrognosisLine.DELETEALL;
      IF UseCostObject THEN BEGIN
        PrognosisLine.SETRANGE("Project No.",Prognosis."Project No.");
        PrognosisLine.SETRANGE("Prognosis Date",Prognosis."Prognosis Date");
        IF PrognosisLine.FIND('-') THEN REPEAT
          TmpPrognosisLine.INIT;
          TmpPrognosisLine.TRANSFERFIELDS(PrognosisLine);
          TmpPrognosisLine.INSERT;
        UNTIL PrognosisLine.NEXT =0;
      END ELSE BEGIN
        PrognosisLineCC.SETRANGE("Project No.",Prognosis."Project No.");
        PrognosisLineCC.SETRANGE("Prognosis Date",Prognosis."Prognosis Date");
        IF PrognosisLineCC.FIND('-') THEN REPEAT
          TmpPrognosisLine.INIT;
          TmpPrognosisLine.TRANSFERFIELDS(PrognosisLineCC);
          TmpPrognosisLine."Cost Object" := PrognosisLineCC."Cost Component Code";
          TmpPrognosisLine.INSERT;
        UNTIL PrognosisLineCC.NEXT =0;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE SpecialCalcForCostComponent@1000000003();
    BEGIN
      IF NOT SpecialCalcForCostComp THEN
        EXIT;
      Sign := -1;

      IF PrevPrognDate <> 0D THEN
        IF PrognosisLineCC.GET(Prognosis."Project No.",PrevPrognDate, '7O') THEN BEGIN
          PrevCostS := (PrognosisLineCC."Prognosis Total Revenues" + PrognosisLineCC."Prognosis Total Cost") * Sign / 1000;
        END;

        PrognosisLineCC.GET(Prognosis."Project No.",Prognosis."Prognosis Date", '7O');
        CostComponent.GET(PrognosisLineCC."Cost Component Code");
        CostCompDescription2 :=TotalLbl + ' ' + CostComponent.Description;
        NewRemainingS := (PrognosisLineCC."Prognosis Costs" + PrognosisLineCC."Prognosis Amount Revenue") * Sign/1000;
        NewTotalS := (PrognosisLineCC."Prognosis Total Cost" + PrognosisLineCC."Prognosis Total Revenues") /1000 * Sign;
        // BUDGET >>
        // Initial Budget >>
        BudgetLine.RESET;
        BudgetLine.SETRANGE("Project No.", PrognosisLineCC."Project No.");
        BudgetLine.SETRANGE(Adjustment,'');
        BudgetLine.SETRANGE("Extension Contract",'');
        BudgetLine.SETRANGE("Version Date",0D, PrognosisLineCC."Prognosis Date");
        BudgetLine.SETRANGE(Option,'');
        BudgetLine.SETRANGE("Cost Component",PrognosisLineCC."Cost Component Code");
        BudgetLine.CALCSUMS("Amount (LCY)");
        OrgBudgetS :=BudgetLine."Amount (LCY)" / 1000 * Sign;

        ProjectInstallment.RESET;
        ProjectInstallment.SETRANGE("Project No.", PrognosisLineCC."Project No.");
        ProjectInstallment.SETFILTER("Extension Contract",'=%1','');
        ProjectInstallment.SETRANGE("Cost Component", PrognosisLineCC."Cost Component Code");
        IF ProjectInstallment.FINDSET THEN REPEAT
          OrgBudgetS += ProjectInstallment."Installment Amount (LCY)" /1000 * Sign;
        UNTIL ProjectInstallment.NEXT=0;

        // Adjustments >>
        BudgetLine.RESET;
        BudgetLine.SETRANGE("Project No.", PrognosisLineCC."Project No.");
        BudgetLine.SETFILTER(Adjustment,'<>%1','');
        BudgetLine.SETRANGE("Extension Contract",'');
        BudgetLine.SETRANGE("Version Date",0D, PrognosisLineCC."Prognosis Date");
        BudgetLine.SETRANGE(Option,'');
        BudgetLine.SETRANGE("Cost Component", PrognosisLineCC."Cost Component Code");
        BudgetLine.CALCSUMS("Amount (LCY)");
        AdjustmentsS :=BudgetLine."Amount (LCY)" / 1000 * Sign;

        // Extensions >>
        BudgetLine.RESET;
        BudgetLine.SETRANGE("Project No.", PrognosisLineCC."Project No.");
        BudgetLine.SETRANGE(Adjustment,'');
        BudgetLine.SETFILTER("Extension Contract",'<>%1','');
        BudgetLine.SETRANGE("Version Date",0D, PrognosisLineCC."Prognosis Date");
        BudgetLine.SETFILTER("Extension Contract Status",'%1|%2',
              BudgetLine."Extension Contract Status"::Order,
              BudgetLine."Extension Contract Status"::"Invoicing Allowed");
        BudgetLine.SETRANGE(Option,'');
        BudgetLine.SETRANGE("Cost Component", PrognosisLineCC."Cost Component Code");
        BudgetLine.CALCSUMS("Amount (LCY)");
        ExtensionsS:=BudgetLine."Amount (LCY)" / 1000 * Sign;

        ProjectInstallment.SETFILTER("Extension Contract",'<>%1','');
        ProjectInstallment.SETRANGE("Cost Component", PrognosisLineCC."Cost Component Code");
        IF ProjectInstallment.FINDSET THEN REPEAT
          ExtensionsS+= ProjectInstallment."Installment Amount (LCY)" /1000 * Sign;
        UNTIL ProjectInstallment.NEXT=0;
        // BUDGET <<

        // ACTUAL / Upparbetat >>
        JobLedgerEntry.SETCURRENTKEY("Job No.", "Posting Date");
        JobLedgerEntry.SETRANGE("Job No.", PrognosisLineCC."Project No.");
        JobLedgerEntry.SETRANGE("Cost Component", PrognosisLineCC."Cost Component Code");
        IF JobLedgerEntry.FIND('-') THEN REPEAT
          CASE JobLedgerEntry."Entry Type" OF
            JobLedgerEntry."Entry Type"::Usage : ActualPostedS += JobLedgerEntry."Total Cost (LCY)" * Sign / 1000;
            JobLedgerEntry."Entry Type"::Sale : ActualPostedS += JobLedgerEntry."Total Price (LCY)" * Sign * -1 / 1000;
          END;
        UNTIL JobLedgerEntry.NEXT=0;

        PurchControlLine.SETCURRENTKEY("Project No.",Date);
        PurchControlLine.SETRANGE("Project No." , PrognosisLineCC."Project No.");
        PurchControlLine.SETRANGE("Cost Component", PrognosisLineCC."Cost Component Code");
        IF PurchControlLine.FIND('-') THEN REPEAT
          ActualOpenS += (PurchControlLine."Outstanding Amount" + PurchControlLine."Amt. Rcd. Not Invoiced")* Sign / 1000;
        UNTIL PurchControlLine.NEXT=0;
        // ACTUAL / Upparbetat <<
    END;

    PROCEDURE ClearVars@1100285011();
    BEGIN
      CLEAR(OrgBudget[1]);
      CLEAR(OrgBudgetH[1]);
      CLEAR(CostComp);
      CLEAR(CostCompDescription);
      CLEAR(Adjustment[1]);
      CLEAR(ActualPosted[1]);
      CLEAR(ActualHours[1]);
      CLEAR(ActualOpen[1]);
      CLEAR(Adjustment[1]);
      CLEAR(AdjustmentsH[1]);
      CLEAR(Extensions[1]);
      CLEAR(ExtensionsH[1]);
      CLEAR(PrevCost[1]);
      CLEAR(PrevHours[1]);
      CLEAR(NewTotal[1]);
      CLEAR(NewHours[1]);
      CLEAR(NewRemaining[1]);
    END;

    PROCEDURE Divide@1100285001(dec1@1100285000 : Decimal;VAR dec2@1100285001 : Decimal);
    BEGIN
      IF dec2 <> 0 THEN
        dec2 := dec1/dec2
      ELSE
        dec2 := 0;
    END;

    PROCEDURE Assign@1100285002(VAR dec1@1100285000 : Decimal;VAR dec2@1100285001 : Decimal);
    BEGIN
      dec1 :=dec2;
    END;

      160412 ITERO.PEPF - Company Name from table "Company Information"
    }

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value = 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function
